       (= -z off)
       (= -h off)
       (= -i off)
       (= -V off)
       (= -R off)
       (= -n off)
       (= --version off)
       (= -g off)
       (= -d off)
       (= --help off)
       (or (and (= -c on) (= -s on) (= --debug off) (= -u off) (= -C off)) a!2))))
